[summaryColumns, setSummaryColumns] = useState({\r\n        index: true,\r\n        site: true,\r\n        wo_no: true,\r\n        wo_date: true,\r\n        wo_value: true,\r\n        bill_certified: true,\r\n        deductions: true,\r\n        paid: true,\r\n        balance: true\r\n    });\r\n    const [showColumnSettings, setShowColumnSettings] = useState(false);\r\n    const [printOrientation, setPrintOrientation] = useState('portrait'); // 'portrait' or 'landscape'\r\n    const [showPrintModal, setShowPrintModal] = useState(false);\r\n\r\n    // Fetch Data\r\n    useEffect(() => {\r\n        const loadInitialData = async () => {\r\n            await fetchData();\r\n\r\n            // Handle URL params for deep linking\r\n            const params = new URLSearchParams(location.search);\r\n            const siteParam = params.get('site');\r\n            const vendorParam = params.get('vendor');\r\n\r\n            if (siteParam) {\r\n                setCurrentView('site_detail');\r\n                setDetailId(siteParam);\r\n            } else if (vendorParam) {\r\n                setCurrentView('vendor_detail');\r\n                setDetailId(vendorParam);\r\n            }\r\n        };\r\n\r\n        loadInitialData();\r\n    }, [location.search]);\r\n\r\n    // Auto-refresh every 30 seconds for Project Overview\r\n    useEffect(() => {\r\n        let intervalId;\r\n        if (readOnly && currentView === 'overview') {\r\n            intervalId = setInterval(() => {\r\n                fetchData(true); // Silent refresh to avoid scroll reset\r\n            }, 30000); // 30 seconds\r\n        }\r\n        return () => {\r\n            if (intervalId) clearInterval(intervalId);\r\n        };\r\n    }, [readOnly, currentView]);\r\n\r\n    const fetchData = async (isSilent = false) => {\r\n        if (!isSilent) setLoading(true);\r\n        try {\r\n            // Corrected Query matching script.js\r\n            const { data, error } = await vendorSupabase\r\n                .from('work_orders')\r\n                .select(`\r\n                    *,\r\n                    sites (name),\r\n                    vendors (vendor_name),\r\n                    advances (*)\r\n                `)\r\n                .order('created_at', { ascending: false });\r\n\r\n            if (error) throw error;\r\n\r\n            // Transform nested relation data into the flat structure required by the UI\r\n            const flattened = (data || []).map(wo => ({\r\n                id: wo.id,\r\n                created_at: wo.created_at,\r\n                site_name: wo.sites?.name || 'Unknown Site',\r\n                vendor_name: wo.vendors?.vendor_name || 'Unknown Vendor',\r\n                wo_no: wo.wo_no,\r\n                wo_date: wo.wo_date,\r\n                wo_value: wo.wo_value,\r\n                bill_certified_value: wo.bill_certified_value,\r\n                housekeeping: wo.housekeeping,\r\n                retention: wo.retention,\r\n                remarks: wo.remarks,\r\n                wo_pdf_url: wo.wo_pdf_url,\r\n                bill_status: wo.bill_status || 'N/A',\r\n                wo_status_url: wo.wo_status_url || '',\r\n                advance_details: wo.advances // Keep as array, code handles it\r\n            }));\r\n\r\n            // Client-side Numerical Sorting by wo_no\r\n            flattened.sort((a, b) => {\r\n                const valA = a.wo_no || '';\r\n                const valB = b.wo_no || '';\r\n                return valA.localeCompare(valB, undefined, { numeric: true, sensitivity: 'base' });\r\n            });\r\n\r\n            setRawData(flattened);\r\n\r\n            // Fetch Master Vendors\r\n            const { data: vData } = await vendorSupabase.from('vendors').select('vendor_name').order('vendor_name');\r\n            setMasterVendors(vData || []);\r\n\r\n            const { data: sData } = await vendorSupabase.from('sites').select('name').order('name');\r\n            setMasterSites(sData || []);\r\n        } catch (error) {\r\n            console.error('Error fetching data:', error);\r\n        } finally {\r\n            if (!isSilent) setLoading(false);\r\n        }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    // Derived Data\r\n    const sites = useMemo(() => {\r\n        const unique = [...new Set(rawData.map(item => item.site_name))];\r\n        return unique.map(site => {\r\n            const siteEntries = rawData.filter(d => d.site_name === site);\r\n            const totalValue = siteEntries.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (parseFloat(item.wo_value) || 0), 0);\r\n            return { name: site, totalValue, count: siteEntries.length, entries: siteEntries };\r\n        });\r\n    }, [rawData]);\r\n\r\n    const vendors = useMemo(() => {\r\n        const vendorMap = {};\r\n        rawData.forEach(item => {\r\n            if (!vendorMap[item.vendor_name]) {\r\n                vendorMap[item.vendor_name] = {\r\n                    name: item.vendor_name,\r\n                    totalValue: 0,\r\n                    advances: 0,\r\n                    sites: new Set(),\r\n                    entries: []\r\n                };\r\n            }\r\n            const v = vendorMap[item.vendor_name];\r\n            v.totalValue += parseFloat(item.wo_value) || 0;\r\n\r\n            let adv = 0;\r\n            try {\r\n                const advList = typeof item.advance_details === 'string' ? JSON.parse(item.advance_details) : item.advance_details;\r\n                if (Array.isArray(advList)) {\r\n                    adv = advList.reduce((acc, curr) => acc + (parseFloat(curr.amount) || 0), 0);\r\n                }\r\n            } catch (e) { }\r\n            v.advances += adv;\r\n            v.sites.add(item.site_name);\r\n            v.entries.push(item);\r\n        });\r\n        return Object.values(vendorMap);\r\n    }, [rawData]);\r\n\r\n    // Format Currency\r\n    const formatCurrency = (amount) => {\r\n        return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-IN', {\r\n            style: 'currency',\r\n            currency: 'INR',\r\n            maximumFractionDigits: 0\r\n        }).format(amount);\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    // formatDate is now imported from utils\r\n\r\n    // Parse Advances safely\r\n    const parseAdvances = (jsonOrArray) => {\r\n        try {\r\n            return typeof jsonOrArray === 'string' ? JSON.parse(jsonOrArray) : (jsonOrArray || []);\r\n        } catch (e) {\r\n            return [];\r\n        }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    // View Navigation\r\n    const handleSwitchView = (view, id = null) => {\r\n        if (readOnly && (view === 'add_entry' || view === 'admin_panel')) return;\r\n        setCurrentView(view);\r\n        if (id) setDetailId(id);\r\n        setSidebarOpen(false);\r\n        setSearchQuery('');\r\n        \r\n        // Scroll content area back to top\r\n        if (contentAreaRef.current) {\r\n            contentAreaRef.current.scrollTo(0, 0);\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // Reset Form if switching away from add_entry\r\n        if (view !== 'add_entry') {\r\n            resetForm();\r\n        }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    const resetForm = () => {\r\n        setEditingState(null);\r\n        setFormData({ siteName: '', vendorName: '', woNo: '', woDate: '', woValue: '', billCertifiedValue: '', housekeeping: '', retention: '', remarks: '', pdfUrl: '', billStatus: 'N/A', woStatusUrl: '' });\r\n        setAdvances([{ amount: '', date: '', payment_mode: 'M1' }]);\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    // --- CRUD Operations ---\r\n\r\n    // 1. Delete\r\n    const handleDelete = async (id) => {\r\n        if (readOnly) return;\r\n        if (!await confirm('Are you sure you want to PERMANENTLY delete this entry?')) return;\r\n        setLoading(true);\r\n        try {\r\n            const { error } = await vendorSupabase.from('work_orders').delete().eq('id', id);\r\n\r\n            if (error) throw error;\r\n            await fetchData();\r\n            toast('Entry deleted.');\r\n        } catch (err) {\r\n            console.error(err);\r\n            await alert('Error deleting entry.');\r\n        } finally {\r\n            setLoading(false);\r\n        }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    // 2. Edit Setup\r\n    const handleEditSetup = (id) => {\r\n        if (readOnly) return;\r\n        const entry = rawData.find(d => d.id === id);\r\n        if (!entry) return;\r\n\r\n        setFormData({\r\n            siteName: entry.site_name,\r\n            vendorName: entry.vendor_name,\r\n            woNo: entry.wo_no,\r\n            woDate: entry.wo_date,\r\n            woValue: entry.wo_value,\r\n            billCertifiedValue: entry.bill_certified_value,\r\n            housekeeping: entry.housekeeping,\r\n            retention: entry.retention,\r\n            remarks: entry.remarks,\r\n            pdfUrl: entry.wo_pdf_url,\r\n            billStatus: entry.bill_status || 'N/A',\r\n            woStatusUrl: entry.wo_status_url || ''\r\n        });\r\n\r\n        const existingAdvances = parseAdvances(entry.advance_details);\r\n        setAdvances(existingAdvances.length > 0 ? existingAdvances : [{ amount: '', date: '', payment_mode: 'M1' }]);\r\n\r\n        setEditingState({ id: entry.id });\r\n        handleSwitchView('add_entry');\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    // 3. Submit (Create/Update)\r\n    const handleSubmit = async (e) => {\r\n        e.preventDefault();\r\n        if (readOnly) return;\r\n\r\n        // Unique Work Order Check\r\n        if (formData.woNo) {\r\n            setLoading(true);\r\n            try {\r\n                let query = vendorSupabase\r\n                    .from('work_orders')\r\n                    .select('id')\r\n                    .eq('wo_no', formData.woNo);\r\n\r\n                if (editingState) {\r\n                    query = query.neq('id', editingState.id);\r\n                }\r\n\r\n                const { data: existingWO, error: checkError } = await query.maybeSingle();\r\n\r\n                if (checkError) throw checkError;\r\n                if (existingWO) {\r\n                    await alert('The work order number already exists');\r\n                    setLoading(false);\r\n                    return;\r\n                }\r\n            } catch (err) {\r\n                console.error('Check error:', err);\r\n                await alert('Error checking work order: ' + err.message);\r\n                setLoading(false);\r\n                return;\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // Site and Vendor Validation\r\n        if (!formData.siteName) {\r\n            await alert('Please Select a Site Name');\r\n            return;\r\n        }\r\n        if (!formData.vendorName) {\r\n            await alert('Please Select a Vendor Name');\r\n            return;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // Work Order Date Validation\r\n        if (!formData.woDate) {\r\n            await alert('Please Fill the Work Order Date Field');\r\n            return;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        setLoading(true);\r\n\r\n        try {\r\n            const finalPdfUrl = formData.pdfUrl;\r\n\r\n            const cleanAdvances = advances.filter(a => a.amount > 0);\r\n\r\n            if (editingState) {\r\n                await updateEntry(editingState.id, formData, finalPdfUrl, cleanAdvances);\r\n            } else {\r\n                await createEntry(formData, finalPdfUrl, cleanAdvances);\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            toast('Saved successfully!');\r\n            await fetchData();\r\n            handleSwitchView('admin_panel');\r\n\r\n        } catch (err) {\r\n            console.error(err);\r\n            const msg = err.message === 'Bucket not found'\r\n                ? 'Storage bucket \"work_orders\" not found. Please create it in your Supabase Dashboard -> Storage.'\r\n                : err.message;\r\n            await alert('Error saving: ' + msg);\r\n        } finally {\r\n            setLoading(false);\r\n        }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    const createEntry = async (data, pdfUrl, advs) => {\r\n        // Find existing Site\r\n        const { data: existingSite } = await vendorSupabase.from('sites').select('id').eq('name', data.siteName).single();\r\n        if (!existingSite) throw new Error(\"Site not found. Please add from Admin.\");\r\n        const siteId = existingSite.id;\r\n\r\n        // Find existing Vendor\r\n        const { data: existingVendor } = await vendorSupabase.from('vendors').select('id').eq('vendor_name', data.vendorName).single();\r\n        if (!existingVendor) throw new Error(\"Vendor not found. Please add from Admin.\");\r\n        const vendorId = existingVendor.id;\r\n\r\n        // Create WO\r\n        const { data: wo, error: woErr } = await vendorSupabase.from('work_orders').insert({\r\n            site_id: siteId,\r\n            vendor_id: vendorId,\r\n            wo_no: data.woNo,\r\n            wo_date: data.woDate,\r\n            wo_value: data.woValue,\r\n            bill_certified_value: data.billCertifiedValue || 0,\r\n            housekeeping: data.housekeeping || 0,\r\n            retention: data.retention || 0,\r\n            remarks: data.remarks,\r\n            wo_pdf_url: pdfUrl,\r\n            bill_status: data.billStatus || 'N/A',\r\n            wo_status_url: data.woStatusUrl\r\n        }).select().single();\r\n        if (woErr) throw woErr;\r\n\r\n        // Create Advances (Manual entries from dashboard)\r\n        if (advs.length > 0) {\r\n            const { error: advErr } = await vendorSupabase.from('advances').insert(\r\n                advs.map(a => ({ work_order_id: wo.id, amount: a.amount, date: a.date, payment_mode: a.payment_mode }))\r\n            );\r\n            if (advErr) throw advErr;\r\n        }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    const updateEntry = async (id, data, pdfUrl, advs) => {\r\n        // Find existing Site\r\n        const { data: newSite } = await vendorSupabase.from('sites').select('id').eq('name', data.siteName).single();\r\n        if (!newSite) throw new Error(\"New Site not found in master records.\");\r\n        const newSiteId = newSite.id;\r\n\r\n        // Find existing Vendor\r\n        const { data: newVendor } = await vendorSupabase.from('vendors').select('id').eq('vendor_name', data.vendorName).single();\r\n        if (!newVendor) throw new Error(\"New Vendor not found in master records.\");\r\n        const newVendorId = newVendor.id;\r\n\r\n        // Update WO\r\n        const { error: woUpdateErr } = await vendorSupabase.from('work_orders').update({\r\n            site_id: newSiteId,\r\n            vendor_id: newVendorId,\r\n            wo_no: data.woNo,\r\n            wo_date: data.woDate,\r\n            wo_value: data.woValue,\r\n            bill_certified_value: data.billCertifiedValue || 0,\r\n            housekeeping: data.housekeeping || 0,\r\n            retention: data.retention || 0,\r\n            remarks: data.remarks,\r\n            wo_pdf_url: pdfUrl, // Update PDF\r\n            bill_status: data.billStatus || 'N/A',\r\n            wo_status_url: data.woStatusUrl\r\n        }).eq('id', id);\r\n        if (woUpdateErr) throw woUpdateErr;\r\n\r\n        // Update Advances (Delete all old, Insert new - simplest strategy)\r\n        await vendorSupabase.from('advances').delete().eq('work_order_id', id);\r\n        if (advs.length > 0) {\r\n            const { error: advErr } = await vendorSupabase.from('advances').insert(\r\n                advs.map(a => ({ work_order_id: id, amount: a.amount, date: a.date, payment_mode: a.payment_mode }))\r\n            );\r\n            if (advErr) throw advErr;\r\n        }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n\r\n    // --- Render Functions ---\r\n\r\n    const renderOverview = () => {\r\n        const totalWOValue = rawData.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (parseFloat(item.wo_value) || 0), 0);\r\n\r\n        return (\r\n            <>\r\n                <div className={styles.statsGrid}>\r\n                    <div className={styles.statCard}>\r\n                        <div className={`${styles.statIcon} ${styles.bgGradient1}`}><Building2 /></div>\r\n                        <div className={styles.statInfo}>\r\n                            <h3>Total Sites</h3>\r\n                            <p>{sites.length}</p>\r\n                        </div>\r\n                    </div>\r\n                    <div className={styles.statCard}>\r\n                        <div className={`${styles.statIcon} ${styles.bgGradient2}`}><Users /></div>\r\n                        <div className={styles.statInfo}>\r\n                            <h3>Active Vendors</h3>\r\n                            <p>{vendors.length}</p>\r\n                        </div>\r\n                    </div>\r\n                    <div className={styles.statCard}>\r\n                        <div className={`${styles.statIcon} ${styles.bgGradient3}`}><FileText /></div>\r\n                        <div className={styles.statInfo}>\r\n                            <h3>Total WO Value</h3>\r\n                            <p>{formatCurrency(totalWOValue)}</p>\r\n                        </div>\r\n                    </div>\r\n                </div>\r\n\r\n\r\n                <h2 className={styles.subtitle} style={{ marginBottom: '1rem', fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '1.2rem' }}>Recent Entries</h2>\r\n                <div className={styles.gridContainer}>\r\n                    {rawData.slice(0, 6).map((item) => (\r\n                        <div key={item.id} className={styles.infoCard}>\r\n                            <div className={styles.cardHeader}>\r\n                                <span>{item.site_name}</span>\r\n                                <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '5px' }}>\r\n                                    <StatusBadge status={item.bill_status} url={item.wo_status_url} />\r\n                                    <span className={styles.tag}>{item.wo_no}</span>\r\n                                </div>\r\n                            </div>\r\n                            <div className={styles.cardBody}>\r\n                                <div className={styles.listItem}>\r\n                                    <span className={styles.listItemTitle}>{item.vendor_name}</span>\r\n                                </div>\r\n                                <div className={styles.listItem}>\r\n                                    <span className={styles.listItemSub}>Work Order Date</span>\r\n                                    <span style={{ fontWeight: 600, color: '#475569' }}>{formatDate(item.wo_date)}</span>\r\n                                </div>\r\n                                <div className={styles.listItem}>\r\n                                    <span className={styles.listItemSub}>WO Value</span>\r\n                                    <span className={styles.currency}>{formatCurrency(item.wo_value)}</span>\r\n                                </div>\r\n                            </div>\r\n                        </div>\r\n                    ))}\r\n                </div>\r\n            </>\r\n        )\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    const renderSites = () => (\r\n        <div className={styles.gridContainer}>\r\n            {sites.filter(s => s.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase())).map(site => (\r\n                <div key={site.name} className={styles.infoCard} onClick={() => handleSwitchView('site_detail', site.name)}>\r\n                    <div className={styles.cardHeader}>\r\n                        <Building2 size={20} />\r\n                        <span>{site.name}</span>\r\n                        <ChevronRight size={16} />\r\n                    </div>\r\n                    <div className={styles.cardBody}>\r\n                        <div className={styles.listItem}>\r\n                            <span className={styles.listItemSub}>Total Value</span>\r\n                            <span className={styles.currency}>{formatCurrency(site.totalValue)}</span>\r\n                        </div>\r\n                        <div className={styles.listItem}>\r\n                            <span className={styles.listItemSub}>Vendors</span>\r\n                            <span style={{ fontWeight: 600 }}>{new Set(site.entries.map(e => e.vendor_name)).size}</span>\r\n                        </div>\r\n                        <div className={styles.tag} style={{ marginTop: '1rem', background: '#eff6ff', color: '#4f46e5' }}>Click for Details</div>\r\n                    </div>\r\n                </div>\r\n            ))}\r\n        </div>\r\n    );\r\n\r\n    const renderVendors = () => (\r\n        <div className={styles.gridContainer}>\r\n            {vendors.filter(v => v.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase())).map(vendor => (\r\n                <div key={vendor.name} className={styles.infoCard} onClick={() => handleSwitchView('vendor_detail', vendor.name)}>\r\n                    <div className={styles.cardHeader}>\r\n                        <Users size={20} />\r\n                        <span>{vendor.name}</span>\r\n                        <ChevronRight size={16} />\r\n                    </div>\r\n                    <div className={styles.cardBody}>\r\n                        <div className={styles.listItem}>\r\n                            <span className={styles.listItemSub}>Total Projects</span>\r\n                            <span className={styles.currency}>{formatCurrency(vendor.totalValue)}</span>\r\n                        </div>\r\n                        <div className={styles.listItem}>\r\n                            <span className={styles.listItemSub}>Active Sites</span>\r\n                            <span>{vendor.sites.size}</span>\r\n                        </div>\r\n                        <div className={styles.tag} style={{ marginTop: '1rem', background: '#eff6ff', color: '#4f46e5' }}>Click for Details</div>\r\n                    </div>\r\n                </div>\r\n            ))}\r\n        </div>\r\n    );\r\n\r\n    const renderSiteDetail = () => {\r\n        const site = sites.find(s => s.name === detailId);\r\n        if (!site) return <div>Site not found</div>;\r\n\r\n        return (\r\n            <div>\r\n                <div className={styles.detailHeader}>\r\n                    <Button variant=\"secondary\" onClick={() => handleSwitchView('sites')}>\r\n                        <ArrowLeft size={16} /> Back to Sites\r\n                    </Button>\r\n                </div>\r\n                <div className={styles.gridContainer}>\r\n                    {site.entries.map(entry => {\r\n                        const allAdvs = parseAdvances(entry.advance_details);\r\n                        const totalAdv = allAdvs.reduce((a, b) => a + (parseFloat(b.amount) || 0), 0);\r\n                        return (\r\n                            <div key={entry.id || Math.random()} className={styles.infoCard} style={{ cursor: 'default' }}>\r\n                                <div className={styles.cardHeader}>\r\n                                    <span>{entry.vendor_name}</span>\r\n                                    <SafePdfBtn url={entry.wo_pdf_url} />\r\n                                </div>\r\n                                <div className={styles.cardBody}>\r\n                                    <div className={styles.listItem}>\r\n                                        <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', width: '100%' }}>\r\n                                            <span className={styles.listItemSub}>Work Order No</span>\r\n                                            <StatusBadge status={entry.bill_status} url={entry.wo_status_url} extraStyles={{ fontSize: '0.7rem', padding: '2px 6px' }} />\r\n\r\n\r\n                                        </div>\r\n                                        <span className={styles.listItemTitle}>{entry.wo_no || 'N/A'}</span>\r\n                                    </div>\r\n                                    <div className={styles.listItem}>\r\n                                        <span className={styles.listItemSub}>Work Order Date</span>\r\n                                        <span style={{ fontWeight: 600, color: '#475569' }}>{formatDate(entry.wo_date)}</span>\r\n                                    </div>\r\n                                    <div className={styles.listItem}>\r\n                                        <span className={styles.listItemSub}>WO Value</span>\r\n                                        <span className={styles.currency}>{formatCurrency(entry.wo_value)}</span>\r\n                                    </div>\r\n                                    <div className={styles.listItem}>\r\n                                        <span className={styles.listItemSub}>Total Paid</span>\r\n                                        <span className={styles.currency} style={{ color: '#4f46e5' }}>{formatCurrency(totalAdv)}</span>\r\n                                    </div>\r\n                                    <div className={styles.listItem}\r\n                                        style={{ background: '#fef2f2', padding: '4px 8px', borderRadius: '4px', marginTop: '4px', cursor: 'pointer' }}\r\n                                        onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); setBalancePopup(entry); }}\r\n                                    >\r\n                                        <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', width: '100%' }}>\r\n                                            <span className={styles.listItemSub} style={{ fontWeight: 600, color: '#b91c1c', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '4px' }}>\r\n                                                Balance to Pay <div style={{ fontSize: '0.7em', border: '1px solid #b91c1c', borderRadius: '50%', width: '14px', height: '14px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' }}>i</div>\r\n                                            </span>\r\n                                            <span className={styles.currency} style={{ fontWeight: 700, color: '#b91c1c' }}>\r\n                                                {formatCurrency((parseFloat(entry.bill_certified_value) || 0) - (parseFloat(entry.housekeeping) || 0) - (parseFloat(entry.retention) || 0) - totalAdv)}\r\n                                            </span>\r\n                                        </div>\r\n                                    </div>\r\n                                    <div style={{ marginTop: '1rem', borderTop: '1px solid #e2e8f0', paddingTop: '0.5rem' }}>\r\n                                        <div style={{     return matchesSearch && matchesDate && matchesMonth && matchesYear && matchesEntity;\r\n        }).sort((a, b) => {\r\n            const woA = a.wo_no || '';\r\n            const woB = b.wo_no ||         );\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        if (statementMode === 'tracker') {\r\n            const vendorGroups = {};\r\n            rawData.forEach(item => {\r\n                const vName =    </div>\r\n                            </div>\r\n                        </div>\r\n                    </div>\r\n                );\r\n\r\n            } else {\r\n                // Simple Delete from Bin\r\n            setSaving(true);\r\n            await supabase.from('recycle_bin').delete().eq('id', binId);\r\n\r\n            // 3. Update State\r\n            setBinItems(binItems.filter(b => b.id !== binId));\r\n            toast('Record restored successfully!');\r\n        } catch (e) {\r\n            await alert(\"Error restoring: \" + e.message);\r\n        } finally { setSaving(false); }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    const permanentDelete = async (binId) => {\r\n        if (await confirm(\"Permanently delete this record? This cannot be undone.\")) {\r\n            setSaving(true);\r\n            try {\r\n                await supabase.from('recycle_bin').delete().eq('id', binId);\r\n                setBinItems(binItems.filter(b => b.id !== binId));\r\n                toast('Record deleted permanently.');\r\n            } catch (e) {\r\n                await alert(\"Error deleting: \" + e.message);\r\n            } finally { setSaving(false); }\r\n        }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    // --- USER MANAGEMENT ACTIONS ---\r\n    const fetchUsers = async () => {\r\n        setSaving(true);\r\n        try {\r\n            const { data, error } = await supabase.from('app_users').select('*').order('username', { ascending: true });\r\n            if (error) throw error;\r\n            setAppUsers(data || []);\r\n        } catch (e) { console.error(e); }\r\n        finally { setSaving(false); }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    const openUserModal = (u = null) => {\r\n        if (u) {\r\n            setEditingUserId(u.id);\r\n            setUserForm({\r\n                username: u.username,\r\n                password: u.password,\r\n                is_admin: u.is_admin,\r\n                permissions: u.permissions || []\r\n            });\r\n        } else {\r\n            setEditingUserId(null);\r\n            setUserForm({ username: '', password: '', is_admin: false, permissions: [] });\r\n        }\r\n        setUserModalOpen(true);\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    const togglePermission = (perm) => {\r\n        const newPerms = userForm.permissions.includes(perm)\r\n            ? userForm.permissions.filter(p => p !== perm)\r\n            : [...userForm.permissions, perm];\r\n        setUserForm({ ...userForm, permissions: newPerms });\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    const saveAppUser = async () => {\r\n        setSaving(true);\r\n        try {\r\n            if (editingUserId) {\r\n                await supabase.from('app_users').update(userForm).eq('id', editingUserId);\r\n            } else {\r\n                await supabase.from('app_users').insert([userForm]);\r\n            }\r\n            setUserModalOpen(false);\r\n            fetchUsers();\r\n            toast(`User account ${editingUserId ? 'updated' : 'created'} successfully!`);\r\n        } catch (e) { await alert(e.message); }\r\n        finally { setSaving(false); }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    const deleteAppUser = async (id) => {\r\n        if (await confirm('Delete this user?')) {\r\n            setSaving(true);\r\n            try {\r\n                await supabase.from('app_users').delete().eq('id', id);\r\n                fetchUsers();\r\n                toast('User deleted successfully!');\r\n            } catch (e) { await alert(e.message); }\r\n            finally { setSaving(false); }\r\n        }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    // --- SETTINGS ACTIONS ---\r\n    const fetchSettings = async () => {\r\n        setSaving(true);\r\n        try {\r\n            const { data, error } = await supabase\r\n                .from('app_settings')\r\n                .select('*')\r\n                .in('setting_key', ['gm_signature_url', 'md_signature_url']);\r\n            if (error) throw error;\r\n            if (data) {\r\n                const gm = data.find(s => s.setting_key === 'gm_signature_url');\r\n                const md = data.find(s => s.setting_key === 'md_signature_url');\r\n                if (gm) setGmSignature(gm.setting_value);\r\n                if (md) setMdSignature(md.setting_value);\r\n            }\r\n        } catch (e) { console.error(e); }\r\n        finally { setSaving(false); }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    const handleSignatureUpload = async (e) => {\r\n        const file = e.target.files[0];\r\n        if (!file) return;\r\n\r\n        setUploading(true);\r\n        try {\r\n            const fileExt = file.name.split('.').pop();\r\n            const fileName = `gm_signature_${Date.now()}.${fileExt}`;\r\n            const filePath = `${fileName}`;\r\n\r\n            // 1. Upload to Supabase Storage\r\n            const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage\r\n                .from('signatures')\r\n                .upload(filePath, file, {\r\n                    contentType: file.type || 'image/png',\r\n                    upsert: true\r\n                });\r\n\r\n            if (uploadError) throw uploadError;\r\n\r\n            // 2. Get Public URL\r\n            const { data: { publicUrl } } = supabase.storage\r\n                .from('signatures')\r\n                .getPublicUrl(filePath);\r\n\r\n            // 3. Update app_settings table\r\n            const { error: dbError } = await supabase\r\n                .from('app_settings')\r\n                .upsert({ setting_key: 'gm_signature_url', setting_value: publicUrl }, { onConflict: 'setting_key' });\r\n\r\n            if (dbError) throw dbError;\r\n\r\n            setGmSignature(publicUrl);\r\n            toast('Signature uploaded successfully!');\r\n        } catch (e) {\r\n            await alert('Upload failed: ' + e.message);\r\n        } finally {\r\n            setUploading(false);\r\n        }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    const handleMdSignatureUpload = async (e) => {\r\n        const file = e.target.files[0];\r\n        if (!file) return;\r\n\r\n        setUploadingMd(true);\r\n        try {\r\n            const fileExt = file.name.split('.').pop();\r\n            const fileName = `md_signature_${Date.now()}.${fileExt}`;\r\n            const filePath = `${fileName}`;\r\n\r\n            const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage\r\n                .from('signatures')\r\n                .upload(filePath, file, {\r\n                    contentType: file.type || 'image/png',\r\n                    upsert: true\r\n                });\r\n\r\n            if (uploadError) throw uploadError;\r\n\r\n            const { data: { publicUrl } } = supabase.storage\r\n                .from('signatures')\r\n                .getPublicUrl(filePath);\r\n\r\n            const { error: dbError } = await supabase\r\n                .from('app_settings')\r\n                .upsert({ setting_key: 'md_signature_url', setting_value: publicUrl }, { onConflict: 'setting_key' });\r\n\r\n            if (dbError) throw dbError;\r\n\r\n            setMdSignature(publicUrl);\r\n            toast('MD Signature uploaded successfully!');\r\n        } catch (e) {\r\n            await alert('Upload failed: ' + e.message);\r\n        } finally {\r\n            setUploadingMd(false);\r\n        }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    // Filter Logic for History\r\n    const filteredHistory = useMemo(() => {\r\n        return history.filter(item => {\r\n            // Status filter\r\n            if (statusFilter !== 'All' && item.status !== statusFilter) return false;\r\n\r\n            // Vendor name filter (case insensitive)\r\n            if (vendorSearch && !item.vendor_name?.toLowerCase().includes(vendorSearch.toLowerCase())) return false;\r\n\r\n            // Date filter\r\n            if (dateSearch && item.date !== dateSearch) return false;\r\n\r\n            // Project/site filter (case insensitive)\r\n            if (projectSearch && !item.project?.toLowerCase().includes(projectSearch.toLowerCase())) return false;\r\n\r\n            return true;\r\n        });\r\n    }, [history, statusFilter, vendorSearch, dateSearch, projectSearch]);\r\n\r\n    const totalAmount = useMemo(() => {\r\n        return filteredHistory.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (parseFloat(item.amount) || 0), 0);\r\n    }, [filteredHistory]);\r\n\r\n    // Clearance List (Only Paid) with filters\r\n    const clearanceList = useMemo(() => {\r\n        return history.filter(h => {\r\n            if (h.status !== 'Paid') return false;\r\n\r\n            // Vendor name filter\r\n            if (vendorSearch && !h.vendor_name?.toLowerCase().includes(vendorSearch.toLowerCase())) return false;\r\n\r\n            // Date filter - Use Paid Date for filtering if available, else standard Date\r\n            if (dateSearch && (h.paid_date !== dateSearch && h.date !== dateSearch)) return false;\r\n\r\n            // Project filter\r\n            if (projectSearch && !h.project?.toLowerCase().includes(projectSearch.toLowerCase())) return false;\r\n\r\n            return true;\r\n        });\r\n    }, [history, vendorSearch, dateSearch, projectSearch]);\r\n\r\n    const clearanceTotal = useMemo(() => {\r\n        return clearanceList.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (parseFloat(item.amount) || 0), 0);\r\n    }, [clearanceList]);\r\n\r\n    // Move to Advances Modal State\r\n    const [showMoveModal, setShowMoveModal] = useState(false);\r\n    const [moveData, setMoveData] = useState({\r\n        item: null,\r\n        date: '',\r\n        mode: 'M1',\r\n        splits: []\r\n    });\r\n\r\n    const openMoveModal = async (item) => {\r\n        const workOrderNo = item.wo_no || item.invoice_no;\r\n        if (!workOrderNo) {\r\n            await alert(\"No Work Order Number associated with this record.\");\r\n            return;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        let initialSplits = Array.isArray(item.payment_splits) ? [...item.payment_splits] : [];\r\n        if (initialSplits.length === 0) {\r\n            initialSplits = [{ amount: item.amount, date: item.paid_date || item.date || new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] }];\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        setMoveData({\r\n            item: item,\r\n            date: item.paid_date || new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0],\r\n            mode: 'M1',\r\n            splits: initialSplits\r\n        });\r\n        setShowMoveModal(true);\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    const confirmMoveToAdvances = async () => {\r\n        const { item, mode, splits } = moveData;\r\n        const workOrderNo = item.wo_no || item.invoice_no;\r\n\r\n        const totalToMove = splits.reduce((sum, s) => sum + (parseFloat(s.amount) || 0), 0);\r\n        if (totalToMove > (parseFloat(item.amount) + 0.01)) { // Allow minor floating point diff\r\n            if (!await confirm(`Total split amount (Γé╣${totalToMove.toLocaleString('en-IN')}) exceeds record amount (Γé╣${parseFloat(item.amount).toLocaleString('en-IN')}). Proceed?`)) return;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        setSaving(true);\r\n        try {\r\n            // Check if WO exists\r\n            const { data: woData, error: woError } = await supabase\r\n                .from('work_orders')\r\n                .select('id')\r\n                .eq('wo_no', workOrderNo)\r\n                .single();\r\n\r\n            if (woError || !woData) {\r\n                await alert(`Work Order Number \"${workOrderNo}\" not registered!`);\r\n                return;\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            const advancesToInsert = splits.map(split => ({\r\n                work_order_id: woData.id,\r\n                amount: parseFloat(split.amount),\r\n                date: split.date,\r\n                payment_mode: mode\r\n            }));\r\n\r\n            // Insert each split as a separate advance\r\n            const { error: advError } = await supabase\r\n                .from('advances')\r\n                .insert(advancesToInsert);\r\n\r\n            if (advError) throw advError;\r\n\r\n            // Mark as moved in history\r\n            const { error: histUpdateErr } = await supabase.from('payment_history').update({ is_moved: true }).eq('id', item.id);\r\n            if (!histUpdateErr) {\r\n                setHistory(prev => prev.filter(h => h.id !== item.id));\r\n            }\r\n            toast(`Successfully moved ${splits.length} split(s) directly to Advances!`);\r\n            setShowMoveModal(false);\r\n        } catch (e) {\r\n            console.error(e);\r\n            toast('Error moving to advances: ' + e.message);\r\n        } finally { setSaving(false); }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    // Vendor search filter\r\n    const [vendorNameSearch, setVendorNameSearch] = useState('');\r\n    const filteredVendors = useMemo(() => {\r\n        return vendors.filter(v =>\r\n            !vendorNameSearch || v.vendor_name?.toLowerCase().includes(vendorNameSearch.toLowerCase())\r\n        );\r\n    }, [vendors, vendorNameSearch]);\r\n\r\n    const filteredSites = useMemo(() => {\r\n        return sites.filter(s =>\r\n            !siteSearch ||\r\n            s.name?.toLowerCase().includes(siteSearch.toLowerCase()) ||\r\n            s.location?.toLowerCase().includes(siteSearch.toLowerCase()) ||\r\n            s.client?.toLowerCase().includes(siteSearch.toLowerCase())\r\n        );\r\n    }, [sites, siteSearch]);\r\n\r\n    const totalPagesHistory = Math.ceil(filteredHistory.length / ROWS_PER_PAGE);\r\n    const paginatedHistory = filteredHistory.slice((currentPage - 1) * ROWS_PER_PAGE, currentPage * ROWS_PER_PAGE);\r\n\r\n    const totalPagesClearance = Math.ceil(clearanceList.length / ROWS_PER_PAGE);\r\n    const paginatedClearance = clearanceList.slice((currentPage - 1) * ROWS_PER_PAGE, currentPage * ROWS_PER_PAGE);\r\n\r\n    const totalPagesVendors = Math.ceil(filteredVendors.length / ROWS_PER_PAGE);\r\n    const paginatedVendors = filteredVendors.slice((currentPage - 1) * ROWS_PER_PAGE, currentPage * ROWS_PER_PAGE);\r\n\r\n    const totalPagesSites = Math.ceil(filteredSites.length / ROWS_PER_PAGE);\r\n    const paginatedSites = filteredSites.slice((currentPage - 1) * ROWS_PER_PAGE, currentPage * ROWS_PER_PAGE);\r\n\r\n    const totalPagesUsers = Math.ceil(appUsers.length / ROWS_PER_PAGE);\r\n    const paginatedUsers = appUsers.slice((currentPage - 1) * ROWS_PER_PAGE, currentPage * ROWS_PER_PAGE);\r\n\r\n    const totalPagesBin = Math.ceil(binItems.length / ROWS_PER_PAGE);\r\n    const paginatedBin = binItems.slice((currentPage - 1) * ROWS_PER_PAGE, currentPage * ROWS_PER_PAGE);\r\n\r\n    if (!isAuthenticated) {\r\n        return (\r\n            <div className={styles.authOverlay}>\r\n                <div className={styles.loginCard}>\r\n                    <h2 className={styles.loginTitle}>Admin Dashboard Login</h2>\r\n                    <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: '15px' }}>\r\n                        <Input\r\n                            placeholder=\"Username\"\r\n                            value={username}\r\n                            onChange={(e) => setUsername(e.target.value)}\r\n                        />\r\n                        <Input\r\n                            type=\"password\"\r\n                            placeholder=\"Password\"\r\n                            value={password}\r\n                            onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}\r\n                            onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleLogin()}\r\n                        />\r\n                    </div>\r\n                    <div style={{ marginTop: '20px' }}>\r\n                        <Button onClick={handleLogin} style={{ width: '100%' }}>Login</Button>\r\n                    </div>\r\n                    {authError && <p style={{ color: 'var(--danger)', marginTop: '10px', textAlign: 'center' }}>Invalid Credentials!</p>}\r\n                </div>\r\n            </div>\r\n        );\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    return (\r\n        <div className={styles.container}>\r\n            {(loadingVendors || loadingHistory || loadingBin || loadingSites || saving) && <LoadingOverlay message={saving ? \"Saving Changes...\" : \"Fetching Data...\"} />}\r\n            {/* Navbar */}\r\n            <div className={styles.topBar}>\r\n                <div className={styles.titleSection}>\r\n                    <h2 className={styles.pageTitle}>Admin Dashboard</h2>\r\n                    <div className={styles.navGroup}>\r\n                        <button\r\n                            className={`${styles.navButton} ${currentView === 'history' ? styles.navButtonActive : ''}`}\r\n                            onClick={() => setCurrentView('history')}\r\n                        >History</button>\r\n                        <button\r\n                            className={`${styles.navButton} ${currentView === 'clearance' ? styles.navButtonActive : ''}`}\r\n                            onClick={() => setCurrentView('clearance')}\r\n                        >Clearance List</button>\r\n                        <button\r\n                            className={`${styles.navButton} ${currentView === 'vendors' ? styles.navButtonActive : ''}`}\r\n                            onClick={() => setCurrentView('vendors')}\r\n                        >Vendors</button>\r\n                        <button\r\n                            className={`${styles.navButton} ${currentView === 'sites' ? styles.navButtonActive : ''}`}\r\n                            onClick={() => setCurrentView('sites')}\r\n                        >Sites</button>\r\n                        <button\r\n                            className={`${styles.navButton} ${currentView === 'bin' ? styles.navButtonActive : ''}`}\r\n                            onClick={() => setCurrentView('bin')}\r\n                        >Recycle Bin</button>\r\n                        {isSuperAdmin && (\r\n                            <>\r\n                                <button\r\n                                    className={`${styles.navButton} ${currentView === 'users' ? styles.navButtonActive : ''}`}\r\n                                    onClick={() => setCurrentView('users')}\r\n                                >Users</button>\r\n                                <button\r\n                                    className={`${styles.navButton} ${currentView === 'settings' ? styles.navButtonActive : ''}`}\r\n                                    onClick={() => setCurrentView('settings')}\r\n                                >Settings</button>\r\n                                <button\r\n                                    className={`${styles.navButton} ${currentView === 'system' ? styles.navButtonActive : ''}`}\r\n                                    onClick={() => { setCurrentView('system'); runDiagnostics(); }}\r\n                                >System Health</button>\r\n                            </>\r\n                        )}\r\n                    </div>\r\n                </div>\r\n                <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '12px', alignItems: 'center' }}>\r\n                    <Link to=\"/\"><Button variant=\"secondary\">Home</Button></Link>\r\n                    <Button variant=\"danger\" onClick={logout}>Logout</Button>\r\n                </div>\r\n            </div>\r\n\r\n            <div className=\"px-6\">\r\n                {/* --- HISTORY VIEW --- */}\r\n                {currentView === 'history' && (\r\n                    <div className={styles.card}>\r\n                        <div className={styles.cardHeader}>\r\n                            <h3 className={styles.cardTitle}>Payment & Invoice History</h3>\r\n                            <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '12px' }}>\r\n                                <button\r\n                                    onClick={fetchHistory}\r\n                                    title=\"Refresh Data\"\r\n                                    style={{\r\n                                        display: 'flex',\r\n                                        alignItems: 'center',\r\n                                        justifyContent: 'center',\r\n                                        width: '40px',\r\n                                        height: '40px',\r\n                                        border: '1px solid #e2e8f0',\r\n                                        borderRadius: '8px',\r\n                                        background: 'white',\r\n                                        cursor: 'pointer',\r\n                                        transition: 'all 0.2s',\r\n                                        color: '#64748b'\r\n                                    }}\r\n                                    onMouseOver={(e) => { e.currentTarget.style.background = '#f1f5f9'; e.currentTarget.style.color = '#334155' }}\r\n                                    onMouseOut={(e) => { e.currentTarget.style.background = 'white'; e.currentTarget.style.color = '#64748b' }}\r\n                                >\r\n                                    ≡ƒöä\r\n                                </button>\r\n                                <button\r\n                                    onClick={clearAllHistory}\r\n                                    title=\"Clear All History\"\r\n                                    style={{\r\n                                        display: 'flex',\r\n                                        alignItems: 'center',\r\n                                        justifyContent: 'center',\r\n                                        width: '40px',\r\n                                        height: '40px',\r\n                                        border: '1px solid #fecaca',\r\n                                        borderRadius: '8px',\r\n                                        background: '#fee2e2',\r\n                                        cursor: 'pointer',\r\n                                        transition: 'all 0.2s',\r\n                                        color: '#b91c1c'\r\n                                    }}\r\n                                    onMouseOver={(e) => e.currentTarget.style.background = '#fecaca'}\r\n                                    onMouseOut={(e) => e.currentTarget.style.background = '#fee2e2'}\r\n                                >\r\n                                    ≡ƒùæ∩╕Å\r\n                                </button>\r\n                                <select\r\n                                    className={styles.statusSelect}\r\n                                    value={statusFilter}\r\n                                    onChange={(e) => setStatusFilter(e.target.value)}\r\n                                    style={{\r\n                                        padding: '8px 12px',\r\n                                        minWidth: '150px',\r\n                                        height: '40px',\r\n                                        border: '1px solid #e2e8f0',\r\n                                        borderRadius: '8px',\r\n                                        background: 'white',\r\n                                        fontWeight: 500\r\n                                    }}\r\n                                >\r\n                                    <option value=\"All\">All Statuses</option>\r\n                                    <option value=\"Pending\">Pending</option>\r\n                                    <option value=\"Approved\">Approved</option>\r\n                                    <option value=\"Partial\">Partial</option>\r\n                                    <option value=\"Paid\">Paid</option>\r\n                                    <option value=\"Rejected\">Rejected</option>\r\n                                </select>\r\n                            </div>\r\n                        </div>\r\n                        <div style={{ padding: '20px 30px', background: '#f8fafc', borderBottom: '1px solid var(--border-color)' }}>\r\n                            <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: '1fr 1fr 1fr', gap: '12px' }}>\r\n                                <input\r\n                                    type=\"text\"\r\n                                    placeholder=\"Search by vendor name...\"\r\n                                    value={vendorSearch}\r\n                                    onChange={(e) => setVendorSearch(e.target.value)}\r\n                                    style={{ padding: '8px 12px', border: '1px solid var(--border-color)', borderRadius: '8px', fontSize: '0.9rem' }}\r\n                                />\r\n                                <input\r\n                                    type=\"date\"\r\n                                    placeholder=\"Filter by date\"\r\n                                    value={dateSearch}\r\n                                    onChange={(e) => setDateSearch(e.target.value)}\r\n                                    style={{ padding: '8px 12px', border: '1px solid var(--border-color)', borderRadius: '8px', fontSize: '0.9rem' }}\r\n                                />\r\n                                <input\r\n                                    type=\"text\"\r\n                                    placeholder=\"Search by project/site...\"\r\n                                    value={projectSearch}\r\n                                    onChange={(e) => setProjectSearch(e.target.value)}\r\n                                    style={{ padding: '8px 12px', border: '1px solid var(--border-color)', borderRadius: '8px', fontSize: '0.9rem' }}\r\n                                />\r\n                            </div>\r\n                        </div>\r\n                        <div className={styles.tableWrapper}>\r\n                            <table className={styles.table}>\r\n                                <thead>\r\n                                    <tr>\r\n                                        <th>Date</th>\r\n                                        <th>Type</th>\r\n                                        <th>Vendor</th>\r\n                                        <th>Project</th>\r\n                                        <th style={{ textAlign: 'right' }}>Total Amount</th>\r\n                                        <th style={{ textAlign: 'right' }}>Paid</th>\r\n                                        <th style={{ textAlign: 'right' }}>Remaining</th>\r\n                                        <th>Status</th>\r\n                                        <th style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>Actions</th>\r\n                                    </tr>\r\n                                </thead>\r\n                                <tbody>\r\n                                    {paginatedHistory.map(item => (\r\n                                        <tr key={item.id}>\r\n                                            <td>{item.date}</td>\r\n                                            <td>\r\n                                                <span className={`${styles.badge} ${item.type === 'invoice' ? styles.badgeInvoice : styles.badgePayment}`}>\r\n                                                    {item.type === 'invoice' ? 'INVOICE' : 'PAYMENT'}\r\n                                                </span>\r\n                                            </td>\r\n                                            <td style={{ fontWeight: 500 }}>{item.vendor_name}</td>\r\n                                            <td>{item.project}</td>\r\n                                            <td style={{ textAlign: 'right', fontWeight: 700 }}>Γé╣{item.amount?.toLocaleString('en-IN')}</td>\r\n                                            <td style={{ textAlign: 'right', color: 'green', fontWeight: 600 }}>\r\n                                                Γé╣{(item.status === 'Paid' ? item.amount : (item.paid_amount || 0)).toLocaleString('en-IN')}\r\n                                            </td>\r\n                                            <td style={{ textAlign: 'right', color: (item.remaining_amount > 0 ? 'red' : 'inherit'), fontWeight: 600 }}>\r\n                                                Γé╣{(item.remaining_amount ?? (item.status === 'Paid' ? 0 : item.amount))?.toLocaleString('en-IN')}\r\n                                            </td>\r\n\r\n                                            <td>\r\n                                                <div style={{ position: 'relative' }}>\r\n                                                    <button\r\n                                                        onClick={(e) => {\r\n                                                            e.stopPropagation();\r\n                                                            setOpenStatusDropdown(openStatusDropdown === item.id ? null : item.id);\r\n                                                        }}\r\n                                                        className={`${styles.statusSelect} ${styles['status' + (item.status || 'Pending')]}`}\r\n                                                        style={{\r\n                                                            width: '100%',\r\n                                                            textAlign: 'left',\r\n                                                            cursor: 'pointer',\r\n         \n            const currentProgress = latestUpdate ? parseFloat(latestUpdate.completion_percentage) : 0;\n            \n            // Calculate Speed (% per day)\n            let speed = 0;\n return parseFloat(val.toFixed(3));\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    const handleAttendanceChange = (laborId, field, value) => {\r\n        setAttendanceEntry(prev => {\r\n            const current = prev[laborId] };\r\n\r\n            const updated = { ...current, [field]: value };\r\n\r\n            // Re-calculate attendance value if times change\r\n            if (field === 'time_in' || field ===     const dailyRate = labors.find(l => l.id === laborId)?.daily_rate || 0;\r\n                updated.wages = parseFloat((updated.attn_val * dailyRate).toFixed(2));\r\n            }\r\n\r\n                    wage_category: r.new_category\r\n                }).eq('id', r.id)\r\n            );\r\n            const results = await Promise.all(updates);\r\n            if (results.some(r => r.error)) throw new Error('Some corrections failed to save.');\r\n            toast('Corrections saved!');\r\n            setCorrectionModalOpen(false);\r\n            fetchWeeklyReport();\r\n        } catch (error) {\r\n            alert(error.message);\r\n        } finally {\r\n            setIsSavingCorrection(false);\r\n        }\r\n    };\r\n\r\n    const deleteCorrectionRecord = async
